<h1 _ngcontent-ghw-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="Tabs"> Tabs </h1>

<div _ngcontent-ghw-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>通过页签进行内容视图切换的容器组件，每个页签对应一个内容视图。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>该组件从API version 7开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p>      <p>该组件从API version 11开始默认支持安全区避让特性(默认值为：expandSafeArea([SafeAreaType.SYSTEM], [SafeAreaEdge.BOTTOM]))，开发者可以重写该属性覆盖默认行为，API version 11之前的版本需配合<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-expand-safe-area">expandSafeArea</a>属性实现安全区避让。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 346px;">     <h2 id="子组件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">子组件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="子组件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>仅支持子组件<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabcontent">TabContent</a>，以及渲染控制类型<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-rendering-control-ifelse" target="_blank">if/else</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-rendering-control-foreach" target="_blank">ForEach</a>，不建议自定义组件作为子组件。并且if/else和ForEach下也仅支持TabContent作为子组件，不建议自定义组件作为子组件。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>Tabs子组件的visibility属性设置为None，或者visibility属性设置为Hidden时，对应子组件不显示，但依然会在视窗内占位。</p>       <p>已经显示的Tabs子组件TabContent后续隐藏时不会被销毁，若需要页面懒加载和释放，可以参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#示例13页面懒加载和释放">示例13</a>。</p>       <p>Tabs设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#height">height</a>为auto时，可根据子组件高度自适应高度大小。设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#width">width</a>为auto时，可根据子组件宽度自适应宽度大小。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 477px;">     <h2 id="接口" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Tabs(options?: TabsOptions)</p>     <p>创建Tabs容器。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#tabsoptions15">TabsOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Tabs组件参数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2604px;">     <h2 id="tabsoptions15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">TabsOptions<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="tabsoptions15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Tabs组件参数，设置Tabs的页签位置，当前显示页签的索引，Tabs控制器和TabBar的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-attributes">通用属性</a>。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.4.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.4.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.4.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.4.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">barPosition<sup>7+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#barposition枚举说明">BarPosition</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置Tabs的页签位置。</p>          <p>默认值：BarPosition.Start。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">index<sup>7+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置当前显示页签的索引。</p>          <p>默认值：0</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>设置为小于0的值时按默认值显示。</p>          <p>可选值为[0, TabContent子节点数量-1]。</p>          <p>直接修改index跳页时，切换动效不生效。 使用TabController的changeIndex时，默认生效切换动效，可以设置animationDuration为0关闭动画。</p>          <p>从API version 10开始，该参数支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-two-way-sync" target="_blank">$$</a>双向绑定变量。</p>          <p>Tabs重建、系统资源切换（如系统字体切换、系统深浅色切换）或者组件属性变化时，会跳转到index对应的页面。若需要在上述情况下不跳转，建议使用双向绑定。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">controller<sup>7+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#tabscontroller">TabsController</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置Tabs控制器。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">barModifier<sup>15+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#commonmodifier15">CommonModifier</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置TabBar的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-attributes">通用属性</a>。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>动态置为undefined时会保持当前状态不变，不会重置各通用属性。</p>          <p>由一个CommonModifier切换为另一个CommonModifier时，重复属性会进行覆盖，非重复属性会同时生效，不会重置前一个CommonModifier的通用属性。</p>          <p>Tabs的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#barwidth">barWidth</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#barheight">barHeight</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#barbackgroundcolor10">barBackgroundColor</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#barbackgroundblurstyle18">barBackgroundBlurStyle</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#barbackgroundeffect18">barBackgroundEffect</a>属性会覆盖CommonModifier的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#width">width</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#height">height</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-background#backgroundcolor18">backgroundColor</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-background#backgroundblurstyle18">backgroundBlurStyle</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-background#backgroundeffect18">backgroundEffect</a>属性。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-location#align">align</a>属性仅在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#barmode10-1">BarMode.Scrollable</a>模式下生效，且Tabs为横向时还需<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#scrollablebarmodeoptions10对象说明">nonScrollableLayoutStyle</a>未设置或设置为异常值时才能生效。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabcontent">TabContent</a>组件的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabcontent#tabbar18">tabBar</a>属性为底部页签样式时不支持拖拽功能。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 504px;">     <h2 id="barposition枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">BarPosition枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="barposition枚举说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Tabs页签位置枚举。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.3.1.1" width="50%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Start</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">vertical属性方法设置为true时，页签位于容器左侧；vertical属性方法设置为false时，页签位于容器顶部。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">End</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">vertical属性方法设置为true时，页签位于容器右侧；vertical属性方法设置为false时，页签位于容器底部。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>除支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-attributes">通用属性</a>外，还支持以下属性：</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 933px;">     <h3 id="vertical" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">vertical<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="vertical" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>vertical(value: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否为纵向Tab。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否为纵向Tab。</p>          <p>默认值：false，横向Tabs，为true时纵向Tabs。</p>          <p>当横向Tabs设置height为auto时，Tabs组件高度自适应子组件高度，即为tabBar高度+divider线宽+TabContent高度+上下padding值+上下border宽度。</p>          <p>当纵向Tabs设置width为auto时，Tabs组件宽度自适应子组件宽度，即为tabBar宽度+divider线宽+TabContent宽度+左右padding值+左右border宽度。</p>          <p>尽量保持每一个页面中的子组件尺寸大小一致，避免滑动页面时出现页面切换动画跳动现象。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 565px;">     <h3 id="scrollable" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">scrollable<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="scrollable" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>scrollable(value: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否可以通过滑动页面进行页面切换。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否可以通过滑动页面进行页面切换。</p>          <p>默认值：true，可以通过滑动页面进行页面切换。为false时不可滑动切换页面。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 634px;">     <h3 id="barmode" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">barMode<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="barmode" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>barMode(value: BarMode, options?: ScrollableBarModeOptions)</p>     <p>设置TabBar布局模式。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#barmode枚举说明">BarMode</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>布局模式。</p>          <p>默认值：BarMode.Fixed</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options<sup>10+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#scrollablebarmodeoptions10对象说明">ScrollableBarModeOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Scrollable模式下的TabBar的布局样式。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>仅Scrollable且水平模式下有效。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 517px;">     <h3 id="barmode10"  </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 973px;">     <h3 id="barwidth" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">barWidth<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="barwidth" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div <p>设置TabBar的宽度值。设置为小于0或大于Tabs宽度值时，按默认值显示。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a><sup>8+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>TabBar的宽度值。</p>          <p>默认值：</p>          <p>未设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabcontent#subtabbarstyle9">SubTabBarStyle</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabcontent#bottomtabbarstyle9">BottomTabBarStyle</a>的TabBar且vertical属性为false时，默认值为Tabs的宽度。</p>          <p>未设置SubTabBarStyle和BottomTabBarStyle的TabBar且vertical属性为true时，默认值为56vp。</p>          <p>设置SubTabBarStyle样式且vertical属性为false时，默认值为Tabs的宽度。</p>          <p>设置SubTabBarStyle样式且vertical属性为true时，默认值为56vp。</p>          <p>设置BottomTabBarStyle样式且vertical属性为true时，默认值为96vp。</p>          <p>设置BottomTabBarStyle样式且vertical属性为false时，默认值为Tabs的宽度。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1141px;">     <h3 id="barheight" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">barHeight<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="barheight" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>barHeight(value: Length)</p>     <p>设置TabBar的高度值。横向Tabs可以设置height为'auto'，让TabBar自适应子组件高度。height设置为小于0或大于Tabs高度值时，按默认值显示。</p>     <p>API version 14之前的版本，若设置barHeight为固定值后，TabBar无法扩展底部安全区。从API version 14开始支持配合<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#safeareapadding14">safeAreaPadding</a>属性，当safeAreaPadding不设置bottom或者bottom设置为0时，可以实现扩展安全区。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>TabBar的高度值。</p>          <p>默认值：</p>          <p>未设置样式或者通过CustomBuilder设置自定义样式的TabBar且vertical属性为false时，默认值为56vp。</p>          <p>未设置样式或者通过CustomBuilder设置自定义样式的TabBar且vertical属性为true时，默认值为Tabs的高度。</p>          <p>设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabcontent#subtabbarstyle9">SubTabBarStyle</a>样式且vertical属性为false时，默认值为56vp。</p>          <p>设置SubTabBarStyle样式且vertical属性为true时，默认值为Tabs的高度。</p>          <p>设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabcontent#bottomtabbarstyle9">BottomTabBarStyle</a>样式且vertical属性为true时，默认值为Tabs的高度。</p>          <p>设置BottomTabBarStyle样式且vertical属性为false时，默认值为56vp，从API version 12开始，默认值变更为48vp。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1282px;">     <h3 id="barheight20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">barHeight<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="barheight20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>barHeight(height: Length, noMinHeightLimit: boolean)</p>     <p>设置TabBar的高度值。横向Tabs可以设置height为'auto'，让TabBar自适应子组件高度，并通过设置noMinHeightLimit为true让自适应高度可以小于TabBar默认高度。height设置为小于0或大于Tabs高度值时，按默认值显示。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead> <p>未设置样式或者通过CustomBuilder设置自定义样式的TabBar且vertical属性为true时，默认值为Tabs的高度。</p>          <p>设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabcontent#subtabbarstyle9">SubTabBarStyle</a>样式且vertical属性为false时，默认值为56vp。</p>          <p>设置SubTabBarStyle样式且vertical属性为true时，默认值为Tabs的高度。</p>          <p>设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabcontent#bottomtabbarstyle9">BottomTabBarStyle</a>样式且vertical属性为true时，默认值为Tabs的高度。</p>          <p>设置BottomTabBarStyle样式且vertical属性为false时，默认值为48vp。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">noMinHeightLimit</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>值为true表示取消TabBar的最小高度限制，即TabBar的高度值可以小于默认值。</p>          <p>值为false表示限制TabBar的最小高度，即TabBar的最小高度值等于默认值。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 829px;">     <h3 id="animationcurve20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">animationCurve<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="animationcurve20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>animationCurve(curve: Curve | ICurve)</p>     <p>设置Tabs翻页动画曲线。常用曲线参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#curve">Curve</a>枚举说明，也可以通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve">插值计算</a>模块提供的接口创建自定义的插值曲线对象。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.16.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">curve</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#curve">Curve</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve#icurve9">ICurve</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Tabs翻页的动画曲线。</p>          <p>默认值：</p>          <p>滑动TabContent翻页时，默认值为interpolatingSpring(-1, 1, 228, 30)。</p>          <p>点击TabBar页签和调用TabsController的changeIndex接口翻页时，默认值为cubicBezierCurve(0.2, 0.0, 0.1, 1.0)。</p>          <p>设置自定义动画曲线时，滑动翻页和点击页签、调用changeIndex翻页都使用设置的动画曲线。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 997px;">     <h3 id="animationduration" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">animationDuration<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="animationduration" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>animationDuration(value: number)</p>     <p>设置Tabs翻页动画时长。</p>     <p>animationCurve不设置时，由于滑动TabContent翻页动画曲线interpolatingSpring(-1, 1, 228, 30)时长只受曲线自身参数影响，animationDuration只能控制点击TabBar页签和调用TabsController的changeIndex接口切换TabContent的动画时长。</p>     <p>不受animationDuration控制的曲线可以查阅<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve">插值计算</a>模块，比如<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve#curvesspringmotion9">springMotion</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve#curvesresponsivespringmotion9">responsiveSpringMotion</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-curve#curvesinterpolatingspring10">interpolatingSpring</a>类型的曲线。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Tabs翻页的动画时长。</p>          <p>默认值：</p>          <p>API version 10及以前，不设置该属性或设置为null时，默认值为0，即Tabs翻页无动画。设置为小于0或undefined时，默认值为300。</p>          <p>API version 11及以后，不设置该属性或设置为异常值，且设置TabBar为BottomTabBarStyle样式时，默认值为0。设置TabBar为其他样式时，默认值为300。</p>          <p>单位：ms</p>          <p>取值范围：[0, +∞)</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 801px;">     <h3 id="animationmode12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">animationMode<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i <p>设置子组件的最大缓存个数和缓存模式。设置该属性后，不会对缓存范围内的子组件进行预加载，仅对缓存范围外的子组件进行释放。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 19开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">所有TabBar平均分配barWidth宽度（纵向时平均分配barHeight高度）。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1017px;">     <h2 id="animationmode12枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">AnimationMode<sup>12+</sup>枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="animationmode12枚举说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>点击TabBar页签时切换TabContent的动画形式枚举。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.4.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.4.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.4.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">CONTENT_FIRST</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>先加载目标页内容，再开始切换动画。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">ACTION_FIRST</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>先开始切换动画，再加载目标页内容；生效需要同时需要满足：Tabs的height、width没有设置成auto。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">NO_ANIMATION</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>关闭默认动画。调用TabsController的changeIndex接口切换TabContent时该枚举值不生效。</p>          <p>可以通过设置animationDuration为0实现调用TabsController的changeIndex接口时不带动画。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">CONTENT_FIRST_WITH_JUMP<sup>15+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">3</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>先加载目标页内容，再无动画跳转到目标页附近，最后有动画跳转到目标页。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">ACTION_FIRST_WITH_JUMP<sup>15+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">4</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>先无动画跳转到目标页附近，再有动画跳转到目标页，最后加载目标页内容。此项生效需要同时需要满足：Tabs的height、width没有设置成auto。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 807px;">     <h2 id="layoutstyle10枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">LayoutStyle<sup>10+</sup>枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Scrollable模式下不滚动时的页签排布方式枚举。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.5.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.5.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.5.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">ALWAYS_CENTER</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>当页签内容超过TabBar宽度时，TabBar可滚动。</p>          <p>当页签内容不超过TabBar宽度时，TabBar不可滚动，页签紧凑居中。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">ALWAYS_AVERAGE_SPLIT</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>当页签内容超过TabBar宽度时，TabBar可滚动。</p>          <p>当页签内容不超过TabBar宽度时，TabBar不可滚动，且所有页签平均分配TabBar宽度。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">SPACE_BETWEEN_OR_CENTER</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>当页签内容超过TabBar宽度时，TabBar可滚动。</p>          <p>当页签内容不超过TabBar宽度但超过TabBar宽度一半时，TabBar不可滚动，页签紧凑居中。</p>          <p>当页签内容不超过TabBar宽度一半时，TabBar不可滚动，保证页签居中排列在TabBar宽度一半，且间距相同。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 449px;">     <h2 id="commonmodifier15" CommonModifier = CommonModifier</p>     <p>作为Tabs组件的参数对象。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p> <h2 id="tabscachemode19枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">TabsCacheMode<sup>19+</sup>枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="tabscachemode19枚举说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>子组件的缓存模式。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 19开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.5.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.5.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.5.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">CACHE_BOTH_SIDE</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">缓存当前显示的子组件和其两侧的子组件。即当设置cachedMaxCount属性的count值为n时，最多缓存2n+1个子组件。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">CACHE_LATEST_SWITCHED</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">缓存当前显示的子组件和最近切换过的子组件。即当设置cachedMaxCount属性的count值为n时，最多缓存n+1个子组件。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="事件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">事件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="事件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>除支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-events">通用事件</a>外，还支持以下事件：</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 833px;">     <h3 id="onchange" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">onChange<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onchange" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onChange(event: Callback&lt;number&gt;)</p>     <p>Tab页签切换后触发的事件。</p>     <p>满足以下任一条件，即可触发该事件：</p>     <p>1、滑动页面进行页面切换时，组件滑动动画结束后触发。</p>     <p>2、通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#tabscontroller">控制器</a>调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#changeindex">changeIndex</a>接口，Tab页签切换后触发。</p>     <p>3、动态修改<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-state" target="_blank">状态变量</a>构造的index属性值，Tab页签切换后触发。</p>     <p>4、点击TabBar页签，Tab页签切换后触发。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>使用自定义页签时，在onChange事件中联动可能会导致滑动页面切换后才执行页签联动，引起自定义页签切换效果延迟。建议在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#onanimationstart11">onAnimationStart</a>中监听并刷新当前索引，以确保动效能够及时触发。具体实现可参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#示例3自定义页签切换联动">示例3</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.13.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.13.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.13.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.13.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">event</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#callback12">Callback</a>&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当前显示的index索引，索引从0开始计算。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 493px;">     <h3 id="ontabbarclick10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onTabBarClick<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="ontabbarclick10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onTabBarClick(event: Callback&lt;number&gt;)</p>     <p>Tab页签点击后触发的事件。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">event</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a 493px;">     <h3 id="onanimationstart11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onAnimationStart<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#animationduration">animationDuration</a>为0时动画关闭且<a align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">handler</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a <h3 id="onanimationend11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onAnimationEnd<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onanimationend11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onAnimationEnd(handler: OnTabsAnimationEndCallback)</p>     <p>切换动画结束时触发该回调，包括动画过程中手势中断。当animationDuration为0时动画关闭，不触发该回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">handler</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#ontabsanimationendcallback18">OnTabsAnimationEndCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">切换动画结束时触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 493px;">     <h3 id="ongestureswipe11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onGestureSwipe<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="ongestureswipe11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onGestureSwipe(handler: OnTabsGestureSwipeCallback)</p>     <p>在页面跟手滑动过程中，逐帧触发该回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">handler</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#ontabsgestureswipecallback18">OnTabsGestureSwipeCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">在页面跟手滑动过程中，逐帧触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 977px;">     <h3 id="customcontenttransition11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">customContentTransition<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="customcontenttransition11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>customContentTransition(delegate: TabsCustomContentTransitionCallback)</p>     <p>自定义Tabs页面切换动画。</p>     <p>使用说明：</p>     <ol>      <li>当使用自定义切换动画时，Tabs组件自带的默认切换动画会被禁用，同时，页面也无法跟手滑动。</li>      <li>当设置为undefined时，表示不使用自定义切换动画，仍然使用组件自带的默认切换动画。</li>      <li>当前自定义切换动画不支持打断。</li>      <li>目前自定义切换动画只支持两种场景触发：点击页签和调用TabsController.changeIndex()接口。</li>      <li>当使用自定义切换动画时，Tabs组件支持的事件中，除了onGestureSwipe，其他事件均支持。</li>      <li>onChange和onAnimationEnd事件的触发时机需要特殊说明：如果在第一次自定义动画执行过程中，触发了第二次自定义动画，那么在开始第二次自定义动画时，就会触发第一次自定义动画的onChange和onAnimationEnd事件。</li>      <li>当使用自定义动画时，参与动画的页面布局方式会改为Stack布局。如果开发者未主动设置相关页面的zIndex属性，那么所有页面的zIndex值是一样的，页面的渲染层级会按照在组件树上的顺序（即页面的index值顺序）确定。因此，开发者需要主动修改页面的zIndex属性，来控制页面的渲染层级。</li>      <li>此属性不支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</li>     </ol>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 20开始，该接口支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">delegate</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#tabscustomcontenttransitioncallback18">TabsCustomContentTransitionCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">自定义Tabs页面切换动画开始时触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 897px;">     <h3 id="oncontentwillchange12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onContentWillChange<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oncontentwillchange12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onContentWillChange(handler: OnTabsContentWillChangeCallback)</p>     <p>自定义Tabs页面切换拦截事件能力，新页面即将显示时触发该回调。</p>     <p>满足以下任一条件，即可触发该事件：</p>     <p>1、滑动TabContent切换新页面时触发。</p>     <p>2、通过TabsController.changeIndex接口切换新页面时触发。</p>     <p>3、通过动态修改index属性值切换新页面时触发。</p>     <p>4、通过点击TabBar页签切换新页面时触发。</p>     <p>5、TabBar页签获焦后，通过键盘左右方向键等切换新页面时触发。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 20开始，该接口支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.14.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.14.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.14.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.14.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">handler</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#ontabscontentwillchangecallback18">OnTabsContentWillChangeCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">自定义Tabs页面切换拦截事件能力，新页面即将显示时触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 753px;">     <h3 id="onselected18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onSelected<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onselected18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onSelected(event: Callback&lt;number&gt;)</p>     <p>当选中元素改变时触发该回调，返回值为当前选中的元素的索引值。</p>     <p>满足以下任一条件，即可触发该事件：</p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>滑动离手时满足翻页阈值，开始切换动画时触发。</p></li>      <li>       <p>通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#tabscontroller">TabsController控制器</a>调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#changeindex">changeIndex</a>接口，开始切换动画时触发。</p></li>      <li>       <p>动态修改<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-state" target="_blank">状态变量</a>构造的index属性值后触发。</p></li>      <li>       <p>通过页签处点击触发。</p></li>     </ol>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#callback12">Callback</a>&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当前选中元素的索引。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 618px;">     <h2 id="ontabsgestureswipecallback18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">OnTabsGestureSwipeCallback<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="ontabsgestureswipecallback18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>Tabs自定义切换动画超时时间。从自定义动画开始切换计时，如果到达该时间后，开发者仍未调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs#tabcontenttransitionproxy11">TabContentTransitionProxy</a>的finishTransition接口通知Tabs组件自定义动画结束，那么组件就会认为此次自定义动画已结束，直接执行后续操作。</p>          <p>默认值：1000</p>          <p>单位：ms</p>          <p>取值范围：[0, +∞)。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">transition</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="tabcontenttransitionproxy11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2> class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Tabs自定义切换动画执行过程中，返回给开发者的proxy对象。开发者可通过该对象获取自定义动画的起始和目标页面信息，同时，也可以通过调用该对象的finishTransition接口通知Tabs组件自定义动画已结束。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>页签在Tabs里的索引值，索引值从0开始。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>设置小于0或大于最大数量的值时，取默认值0。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1111px;">     <h3 id="preloaditems12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">preloadItems<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="preloaditems12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>preloadItems(indices: Optional&lt;Array&lt;number&gt;&gt;): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>控制Tabs预加载指定子节点。调用该接口后会一次性加载所有指定的子节点，因此为了性能考虑，建议分批加载子节点。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>Tabs的preloadItems需要在Tabs创建之后去调用，首次预加载推荐在Tabs的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-events-show-hide#onappear">onAppear</a>生命周期中去控制。</p></li>        <li>         <p>如果TabsController对象未绑定任何Tabs组件，直接调用该接口，会抛出JS异常。因此使用该接口时，建议通过try-catch捕获异常。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.62.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.62.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.62.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.62.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">indices</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Optional&lt;Array&lt;number&gt;&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>需预加载的子节点的下标数组。</p>          <p>默认值：空数组。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.62.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.62.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;void&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">预加载完成后触发的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.62.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.62.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter invalid. Possible causes: 1. The parameter type is not Array&lt;number&gt;; 2. The parameter is an empty array; 3. The parameter contains an invalid index.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 609px;">     <h3 id="settabbartranslate13" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setTabBarTranslate<sup>13+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="settabbartranslate13" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setTabBarTranslate(translate: TranslateOptions): void</p>     <p>设置TabBar的平移距离。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-uicontext-uicontext#bindtabstoscrollable13">bindTabsToScrollable</a>或<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-uicontext-uicontext#bindtabstonestedscrollable13">bindTabsToNestedScrollable</a>等接口绑定了Tabs组件和可滚动容器组件后，在滑动可滚动容器组件时，会触发所有与其绑定的Tabs组件的TabBar的显示和隐藏动效，调用setTabBarTranslate接口设置的TabBar平移距离会失效。因此不建议同时使用bindTabsToScrollable、bindTabsToNestedScrollable和setTabBarTranslate接口。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 13开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.63.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.63.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.63.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.63.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">translate</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-transformation#translateoptions对象说明">TranslateOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">设置TabBar的平移距离。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 729px;">     <h3 id="settabbaropacity13" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setTabBarOpacity<sup>13+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="settabbaropacity13" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setTabBarOpacity(opacity: number): void</p>     <p>设置TabBar的不透明度。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-uicontext-uicontext#bindtabstoscrollable13">bindTabsToScrollable</a>或<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-uicontext-uicontext#bindtabstonestedscrollable13">bindTabsToNestedScrollable</a>等接口绑定了Tabs组件和可滚动容器组件后，在滑动可滚动容器组件时，会触发所有与其绑定的Tabs组件的TabBar的显示和隐藏动效，调用setTabBarOpacity接口设置的TabBar不透明度会失效。因此不建议同时使用bindTabsToScrollable、bindTabsToNestedScrollable和setTabBarOpacity接口。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 13开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">opacity</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置TabBar的不透明度，取值范围为[0.0, 1.0]，设置的值小于0.0时，按0.0处理，设置的值大于1.0时，按1.0处理。</p>          <p>默认值：1.0。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 146px;">     <h2 id="示例" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">示例<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="示例" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>         <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2464px;">     <h3 id="示例1设置tabbar的布局模式" class="firsth2">示例1（设置TabBar的布局模式）<i </li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">getCurrentIndicatorInfo</span>(<span class="hljs-attr">index</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">event</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">TabsAnimationEvent</span>): <span class="hljs-title class_">Record</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">string</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>&gt; {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> nextIndex = index;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (index &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> &amp;&amp; (<span class="hljs-title class_">CommonUtil</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getIsRTL</span>() ? event.<span class="hljs-property">currentOffset</span> &lt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> : event.<span class="hljs-property">currentOffset</span> &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)) {</li><li>      nextIndex--;</li><li>    } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (index &lt; <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">textInfos</span>.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> - <span class="hljs-number">1</span> &amp;&amp;</li><li>        (<span class="hljs-title class_">CommonUtil</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getIsRTL</span>() ? event.<span class="hljs-property">currentOffset</span> &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> : event.<span class="hljs-property">currentOffset</span> &lt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)) {</li><li>      nextIndex++;</li><li>    }</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> indexInfo = <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">textInfos</span>[index];</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> nextIndexInfo = <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">textInfos</span>[nextIndex];</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> swipeRatio = <span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">abs</span>(event.<span class="hljs-property">currentOffset</span> / <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">tabsWidth</span>);</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> currentIndex = swipeRatio &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0.5</span> ? nextIndex : index; <span class="hljs-comment">// 页面滑动超过一半，tabBar切换到下一页。</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> currentLeft = indexInfo[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>] + (nextIndexInfo[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>] - indexInfo[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]) * swipeRatio;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> currentWidth = indexInfo[<span class="hljs-number">1</span>] + (nextIndexInfo[<span class="hljs-number">1</span>] - indexInfo[<span class="hljs-number">1</span>]) * swipeRatio;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> { <span class="hljs-string">'index'</span>: currentIndex, <span class="hljs-string">'left'</span>: currentLeft, <span class="hljs-string">'width'</span>: currentWidth };</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">startAnimateTo</span>(<span class="hljs-params">duration: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, leftMargin: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, width: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">isStartAnimateTo</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>;</li><li>    <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getUIContext</span>()?.<span class="hljs-title function_">animateTo</span>({</li><li>      <span class="hljs-attr">duration</span>: duration, <span class="hljs-comment">// 动画时长</span></li><li>      <span class="hljs-attr">curve</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Curve</span>.<span class="hljs-property">Linear</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// 动画曲线</span></li><li>      <span class="hljs-attr">iterations</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// 播放次数</span></li><li>      <span class="hljs-attr">playMode</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">PlayMode</span>.<span class="hljs-property">Normal</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// 动画模式</span></li><li>      <span class="hljs-attr">onFinish</span>: <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {</li><li>        <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">isStartAnimateTo</span> = <span class="hljs-literal">false</span>;</li><li>        <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'play end'</span>);</li><li>      }</li><li>    }, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {</li><li>      <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setIndicatorAttr</span>(leftMargin, width);</li><li>    });</li><li>  }</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">setIndicatorAttr</span>(<span class="hljs-params">leftMargin: <span class="hljs-built_in">number</span>, width:
